          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }

          flex-wrap: no-wrap;

        }

          width: 100%;

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>

        <p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Steps to reproduce the problem:



<span class="line"><!---->Steps to reproduce the problem:<!----></span>



<br>





1. download chromium-asan-887050.zip and unzip



<span class="line"><!---->1. download chromium-asan-887050.zip and unzip<!----></span>



<br>





2. `touch no.js` at the same folder of poc.html and start a server `python -m SimpleHTTPServer 8605`



<span class="line"><!---->2. `touch no.js` at the same folder of poc.html and start a server `python -m SimpleHTTPServer 8605`<!----></span>



<br>





3. "close the network" and ./chrome 



<span class="line"><!---->3. "close the network" and ./chrome <!----></span>





http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html"><!---->http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html<!----></a>



<br>





4. click cancel of download item



<span class="line"><!---->4. click cancel of download item<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





What is the expected behavior?



<span class="line"><!---->What is the expected behavior?<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





What went wrong?



<span class="line"><!---->What went wrong?<!----></span>



<br>





In function CancelDownload[1] of file components/background_fetch/background_fetch_delegate_base.cc 



<span class="line"><!---->In function CancelDownload[1] of file components/background_fetch/background_fetch_delegate_base.cc <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Call to Abort [2] will re-assign offline_item_ and free the older offline_item_, however the function GetClient[3] will use it again => UAF.



<span class="line"><!---->Call to Abort [2] will re-assign offline_item_ and free the older offline_item_, however the function GetClient[3] will use it again =&gt; UAF.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>

<br>

<span class="line"><!---->  DCHECK_CURRENTLY_ON(content::BrowserThread::UI);<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->  JobDetails* job_details = GetJobDetails(job_id);<!----></span>

<br>





      job_details->job_state == JobDetails::State::kJobComplete) {



<span class="line"><!---->      job_details-&gt;job_state == JobDetails::State::kJobComplete) {<!----></span>



<br>





    // The cancel event arrived after the fetch was complete; ignore it.



<span class="line"><!---->    // The cancel event arrived after the fetch was complete; ignore it.<!----></span>



<br>





    return;



<span class="line"><!---->    return;<!----></span>



<br>





  }



<span class="line"><!---->  }<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  job_details->cancelled_from_ui = true;



<span class="line"><!---->  job_details-&gt;cancelled_from_ui = true;<!----></span>



<br>





  Abort(job_id);



<span class="line"><!---->  Abort(job_id);<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  if (auto client = GetClient(job_id)) {



<span class="line"><!---->  if (auto client = GetClient(job_id)) {<!----></span>



<br>





    client->OnJobCancelled(



<span class="line"><!---->    client-&gt;OnJobCancelled(<!----></span>



<br>





        job_id, blink::mojom::BackgroundFetchFailureReason::CANCELLED_FROM_UI);



<span class="line"><!---->        job_id, blink::mojom::BackgroundFetchFailureReason::CANCELLED_FROM_UI);<!----></span>

  }



<span class="line"><!---->  }<!----></span>

}

Reproduced on Mac ASAN build 887050 as follows.



<span class="line"><!---->Reproduced on Mac ASAN build 887050 as follows.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1. Put poc.html in a folder



<span class="line"><!---->1. Put poc.html in a folder<!----></span>



<br>





2. touch no.js



<span class="line"><!---->2. touch no.js<!----></span>



<br>





3. python3 -m http.server 8605



<span class="line"><!---->3. python3 -m http.server 8605<!----></span>



<br>





4. Open Chromium and visit 



<span class="line"><!---->4. Open Chromium and visit <!----></span>





http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html"><!---->http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html<!----></a>





,



<span class="line"><!---->,<!----></span>





 wait for the background fetch to complete



<span class="line"><!----> wait for the background fetch to complete<!----></span>



<br>





5. Quit Chromium



<span class="line"><!---->5. Quit Chromium<!----></span>



<br>





6. From the command line run Chromium.app/Contents/MacOS/Chromium 



<span class="line"><!---->6. From the command line run Chromium.app/Contents/MacOS/Chromium <!----></span>





http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html"><!---->http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html<!----></a>



<br>





7. On the keychain dialog which appears, click Deny (or presumably any other option)



<span class="line"><!---->7. On the keychain dialog which appears, click Deny (or presumably any other option)<!----></span>



<br>





8. Immediately as soon as the window appears, you'll see the download start in the bottom left.



<span class="line"><!---->8. Immediately as soon as the window appears, you'll see the download start in the bottom left.<!----></span>



<br>





9. Immediately click on the pop-up menu and choose Cancel



<span class="line"><!---->9. Immediately click on the pop-up menu and choose Cancel<!----></span>



<br>





10. Get ASAN crash as below.



<span class="line"><!---->10. Get ASAN crash as below.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This seems to be subtly different from the Linux instructions: on the Mac, the download completes almost immediately even if WiFi is off. You have to strike fast to cancel the download before it's too late.



<span class="line"><!---->This seems to be subtly different from the Linux instructions: on the Mac, the download completes almost immediately even if WiFi is off. You have to strike fast to cancel the download before it's too late.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In fact there seems to be no point turning off wifi on the Mac - it is equally reproducible with and without the network on, but you have to act fast to cancel the download.



<span class="line"><!---->In fact there seems to be no point turning off wifi on the Mac - it is equally reproducible with and without the network on, but you have to act fast to cancel the download.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





As a browser process bug triggered by web content, this would normally be Critical severity. But I'm assuming that the UI interaction of cancelling the download here is a necessary part of the reproduction and thus I'm downgrading this to High. merc.ouc@, if you know any way to trigger this without UI gestures please let us know.



<span class="line"><!---->As a browser process bug triggered by web content, this would normally be Critical severity. But I'm assuming that the UI interaction of cancelling the download here is a necessary part of the reproduction and thus I'm downgrading this to High. merc.ouc@, if you know any way to trigger this without UI gestures please let us know.<!----></span>

A few thoughts -



<span class="line"><!---->A few thoughts -<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  (1) GetJobDetails() uses NOTREACHED() to catch the case where no job details can be found, but that's substituted by DCHECK(false) and therefore removed in release builds. That should be a fatal check, or we bail out on nullptrs in CancelDownload() like we do in the other methods.



<span class="line"><!---->  (1) GetJobDetails() uses NOTREACHED() to catch the case where no job details can be found, but that's substituted by DCHECK(false) and therefore removed in release builds. That should be a fatal check, or we bail out on nullptrs in CancelDownload() like we do in the other methods.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  (2) The stack trace about usage misses a whole bunch of steps between #3 and #4 -- more than I would expect. I don't actually see where the UAF is happening. +shaktisahu and +rayankans, could you take a look please?



<span class="line"><!---->  (2) The stack trace about usage misses a whole bunch of steps between #3 and #4 -- more than I would expect. I don't actually see where the UAF is happening. +shaktisahu and +rayankans, could you take a look please?<!----></span>

Sorry, I just got around to this.



<span class="line"><!---->Sorry, I just got around to this.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I'm not 100% sure what's happening here (I'm unable to reproduce), but from investigating the stack trace + code here are a few comments.



<span class="line"><!---->I'm not 100% sure what's happening here (I'm unable to reproduce), but from investigating the stack trace + code here are a few comments.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1. The |ui_state_map_|  and |job_details_map_| always erase entries together.



<span class="line"><!---->1. The |ui_state_map_|  and |job_details_map_| always erase entries together.<!----></span>



<br>





2. Looking at the duplicate stack traces 2 & 3, it looks like we are receiving a delayed update event (BackgroundFetchDelegateImpl::DoUpdateUi) after the job has been marked as complete. An invalid offline_item is then sent to OfflineItemModel::OnItemUpdated, which invokes the copy constructor on invalid data. I sent a fix here  



<span class="line"><!---->2. Looking at the duplicate stack traces 2 &amp; 3, it looks like we are receiving a delayed update event (BackgroundFetchDelegateImpl::DoUpdateUi) after the job has been marked as complete. An invalid offline_item is then sent to OfflineItemModel::OnItemUpdated, which invokes the copy constructor on invalid data. I sent a fix here  <!----></span>





https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/2983039



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/2983039"><!---->https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/2983039<!----></a>



<br>





3. I have no idea what's happening in stack trace #1. Both repros by merc.ouc@ and adetaylor@ suggest something is going wrong when accessing an item |job_details_map_| in BackgroundFetchDelegateBase::CancelDownload. According to the stack trace from merc.ouc@ this is happening when `GetClient` is called, however that is safe and we check for nullptrs there. We also don't modify the map states at any point in between. I'm wondering if this is also a delayed cancel event when the maps have already been cleared (aborting from the UI after the fetch is & clean-up is complete), and the UAF is happening when we check the job state. I sent a fix for that here: 



<span class="line"><!---->3. I have no idea what's happening in stack trace #1. Both repros by merc.ouc@ and adetaylor@ suggest something is going wrong when accessing an item |job_details_map_| in BackgroundFetchDelegateBase::CancelDownload. According to the stack trace from merc.ouc@ this is happening when `GetClient` is called, however that is safe and we check for nullptrs there. We also don't modify the map states at any point in between. I'm wondering if this is also a delayed cancel event when the maps have already been cleared (aborting from the UI after the fetch is &amp; clean-up is complete), and the UAF is happening when we check the job state. I sent a fix for that here: <!----></span>





https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/2982462



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/2982462"><!---->https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/2982462<!----></a>

<span class="line"><!---->Now that we have eliminated event orders from potentially causing this, it looks like this is being caused by:<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->- the cancel flow sending a reference to the offline item<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->- the update flow overwriting the offline item<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

1. Does your merge fit within the Merge Decision Guidelines?

- Chrome:

<span class="line"><!---->2. Links to the CLs you are requesting to merge.<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.
